#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x000B [0x20] SET_CLI_EVENT_UC_FLAG: Lock player control
  1: 0x000D [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  2: 0x000F [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  3: 0x0010 [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
```
